### Line of Ulkhash

	    birth = yes

	    trait = vengeful

	}
	6796.04.28 = {
		trait = maimed

			add_character_flag = {	
				flag = had_nickname_event
			}	
		}
	}

	}
	6958.11.21 = {  # Died at age 192
	    death = { death_reason = death_maimed }
	}
}

##### Line of Hargash ###
lineofhargash1 = {	#LW Ruler- Orc Haesteinn easter egg
	name = Hargrog
	dynasty = dynasty_hargash
	religion = faith_peltripper
	culture = rukhashai
	diplomacy = 9
	martial = 9
	stewardship = 5
	intrigue = 7
	learning = 4
	health = 6.5
	trait = intellect_good_1
	trait = whole_of_body
	sexuality = heterosexual
	disallow_random_traits = yes
	6735.1.1 = {
		birth = yes
		effect = {
			#add_character_flag = has_scripted_appearance
			# Sort his perk tree out.
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_perk = anatomical_studies_perk } }
				add_perk = anatomical_studies_perk
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_perk = restraint_perk } }
				add_perk = restraint_perk
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_perk = know_thyself_perk } }
				add_perk = know_thyself_perk
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_perk = wash_your_hands_perk } }
				add_perk = wash_your_hands_perk
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_perk = iron_constitution_perk } }
				add_perk = iron_constitution_perk
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_perk = healthy_perk } }
				add_perk = healthy_perk
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_perk = whole_of_body_perk } }
				add_perk = whole_of_body_perk
			}
		}	
	}
	6751.1.1 = {
		trait = lustful
		trait = ambitious
		trait = greedy
		trait = education_martial_4
	}
	6785.1.1 = {
		trait = viking
		trait = adventurer
		give_nickname = nick_the_hasty
		effect = {
			add_character_flag = had_nickname_event
		}
		#add_character_modifier = orc_lust_for_adventure_modifier	#Add in his starting event
		effect = {		
			add_gold = 500
			add_prestige = 2000 # Rich and prestigious from raiding
			add_prestige_experience = 5000 # So that we have enough prestige to use an invasion CB
		}
	}
	6816.1.1 = {
	    death = { death_reason = death_fallen_from_a_mountain }
	}
}
